### [169] [Staleness-Learning Rate Scaling Laws for Asynchronous RLHF](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01083)
*Jingwei Song,Haofeng Xu,Jie Xiao,Chengke Bao,Jingwei Shi,Pengbin Feng,Weixun Wang,Yuhang Han,Chuan Wu,Linfeng Zhang,Bill Shi*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文理论分析了异步GRPO中陈旧rollout（滞后S步）导致的梯度偏差为O(S·η)，并推导出稳定性条件依赖于min{R_batch/(S·G_upd), R_crit/(T·η)}，解释了学习率对滞后程度的弱依赖性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高吞吐RLHF系统中，rollout生成与策略优化解耦导致陈旧数据使用，现有工作缺乏对陈旧性在异步GRPO中影响的理论分析。

Method: 显式区分行为策略与目标策略，将陈旧性建模为行为策略滞后；通过局部有界性、分布平滑性和行为策略平滑性假设，推导陈旧rollout引入的梯度偏差阶数；进一步推导条件性坍塌时间标度律，给出两约束稳定性条件。

Result: 陈旧rollout引入每步O(S·η)的代理梯度偏差；在循环内漂移低于批次裁剪半径时，坍塌由累积学习者漂移T·η主导；陈旧rollout约束激活时，稳定性由S·η决定；最终稳定性条件为η << min{R_batch/(S·G_upd), R_crit/(T·G_upd)}。

Conclusion: 最大稳定学习率在horizon受限情况下可能对陈旧性呈现弱依赖性，为实际异步RLHF系统的超参数设置提供了理论依据。

Abstract: High-throughput RLHF systems often decouple rollout generation from policy optimization, leading to the use of stale rollouts during learner updates. In this work, we study the effect of such staleness in asynchronous GRPO. We make the behavior policy explicit in the GRPO surrogate objective and distinguish between the surrogate-gradient mapping used by the learner and the true total derivative of a distribution-dependent population objective. Under assumptions of local boundedness, distributional smoothness, and behavior-policy smoothness, we show that stale rollouts introduce a per-step surrogate-gradient bias of order O(S * eta), where S denotes the maximum rollout lag and eta denotes the learning rate. We further derive a conditional collapse-time scaling law: when within-cycle drift remains below a batch-level clipping radius, collapse is governed primarily by cumulative learner drift T * eta; when the stale-rollout constraint is active, stability instead depends explicitly on S * eta. This yields a two-constraint stability condition eta << min{R_batch / (S * G_upd), R_crit / (T * G_upd)}, explaining why the maximum stable learning rate may appear weakly dependent on staleness in the horizon-limited regime.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 将数据混合优化形式化为因果推断问题：以数据池统计特征为协变量，领域混合比例为处理变量；在Qwen2.5-0.5B上进行512次运行拟合因果模型估计CATE，然后外推最优混合比例用于800K数据池训练7B模型；并成功泛化到Qwen3-4B-Base的长思维链数据上。

Abstract: In Large Language Model (LLM) training, data mixing plays a pivotal role in determining model performance. Recent methods optimize mixture weights via proxy models, but they rely on the assumption of static data distributions. As a result, when the underlying data pool shifts, these methods require costly retraining from scratch. This limitation restricts their ability to scale seamlessly from small settings to larger data pools and model sizes. In this paper, we propose CausalMix to address this limitation by casting data mixture optimization as a causal inference problem. We formulate the statistical features of the data pool as covariates and the domain mixture as the treatment. After fitting a causal model on 512 runs of Qwen2.5-0.5B to estimate the Conditional Average Treatment Effect (CATE), we extrapolate the optimal mixture for an 800K data pool and apply it to train a 7B model. Furthermore, we successfully generalize the framework to long chain-of-thought data on Qwen3-4B-Base. By leveraging causal modeling to isolate confounding biases, CausalMix dynamically infers state-dependent optimal data mixtures. Extensive experiments show that the mixture guided by CausalMix consistently improves performance across multiple downstream tasks, outperforming RegMix and other baselines. In addition, we use the CATE Interpreter to provide visual analysis of the learned mixing strategy. Overall, CausalMix offers a causal and interpretable framework for optimizing LLM data mixtures.

### [171] [QuasiMoTTo: Quasi-Monte Carlo Test-Time Scaling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01179)
*Michael Y. Li,Anthony Zhan,Kanishk Gandhi,Noah D. Goodman,Emily B. Fox*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: QuasiMoTTo通过拟蒙特卡洛方法生成相关但边缘分布正确的样本，替代独立同分布采样，在推理和强化学习中用更少样本达到同等性能（pass@k减少25-47%，GRPO训练步数减少50%）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 缩放推理计算时，独立同分布采样会产生大量冗余解，浪费计算资源。作者认为独立性与样本效率之间的权衡并非不可打破，因此希望探索相关采样设计空间来提高样本效率。

Method: 将自回归采样重参数化为逆CDF采样，用拟蒙特卡洛（QMC）生成更均匀分布的基础随机数，从而产生边缘分布正确但整体相关的样本。同时开发了无偏bootstrap估计器替代被相关性破坏的pass@k估计。

Result: 在四个推理基准上，QuasiMoTTo以25-47%更少样本匹配i.i.d.的pass@k精度，且常达到边缘保留采样器的pass@k理论上界。在GRPO中，以50%更少训练步数匹配i.i.d.性能。

Conclusion: 相关采样能有效提高计算到性能的转化效率，核心优势在于更均匀的覆盖带来更强的每批次学习信号，且不改变样本的边缘分布，可直接用于策略梯度训练。

Abstract: Scaling inference compute, by generating many parallel attempts per problem, is a costly but reliable lever for improving language model capabilities. By default these attempts are generated independently, wasting inference compute on redundant solutions. This waste seems unavoidable. After all, independence is what makes parallel sampling trivial to scale. However, this tradeoff is not fundamental: there is a rich design space of samplers that generate correlated but exact samples entirely in parallel. We explore this design space as an avenue for improving sample efficiency in scaling inference compute and reinforcement learning (RL). Concretely, we introduce QuasiMoTTo, which uses correlated samples as a drop-in replacement for i.i.d. samples. To generate these samples, QuasiMoTTo uses a reparameterization of autoregressive sampling as inverse-CDF sampling and draws the underlying uniforms with quasi-Monte Carlo (QMC); because QMC spreads the uniforms out more evenly than i.i.d., the resulting samples cover the output space with far less redundancy. Even though the batch is correlated, each sample is marginally distributed according to the language model, so we can use the batch for policy-gradient training. Our empirical analysis focuses on understanding how efficiently QuasiMoTTo can turn compute into performance. To evaluate correlated samplers, whose dependence breaks standard pass@k estimators, we first develop an unbiased bootstrap estimator. Across four reasoning benchmarks, QuasiMoTTo matches i.i.d. pass@k accuracy with 25-47% fewer samples. Strikingly, QuasiMoTTo often saturates an upper bound on pass@k that holds for any marginal-preserving sampler. We also apply QuasiMoTTo to policy-gradient RL (GRPO) where it matches i.i.d. performance with 50% fewer training steps. These gains come from higher coverage, which yields a stronger learning signal per batch.

</details>

TL;DR: 本文系统地研究了强化学习后训练在Transformer各层中的分布情况，发现单层训练即可恢复甚至超越全参数RL训练的大部分收益，且高贡献层集中在transformer堆栈的中部。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法通常对所有模型参数进行均匀更新，隐含假设每一层对RL后训练的贡献相同。作者挑战这一假设，希望理解RL适应在Transformer各层中的分布规律。

Method: 通过逐层隔离训练的方式，引入"层贡献度"（layer contribution）指标，量化单独训练某一层所能恢复的全参数RL训练收益比例。在7个模型（Qwen3、Qwen2.5系列）、3种RL算法（GRPO、GiGPO、Dr. GRPO）及多个任务领域上系统验证。

Result: RL训练收益高度集中于少数甚至单个Transformer层；高贡献层集中在transformer堆栈的中部，而输入输出端附近的层贡献显著较低；层排名在不同数据集、任务、模型族和RL算法间高度一致。

Conclusion: RL后训练的收益在Transformer中呈现出显著的集中性和结构化分布模式，挑战了均匀更新的传统假设，为更高效的微调策略提供启示。

Abstract: Reinforcement learning (RL) has become a central component of post-training large language models (LLMs), yet little is understood about how RL adaptation is distributed across transformer layers. Existing approaches typically update all model parameters uniformly, implicitly assuming that every layer contributes similarly to the gains obtained during RL post-training. In this work, we challenge this assumption through a systematic layer-wise study of RL training. Surprisingly, we find that training a single transformer layer can recover most of the gains achieved by full-parameter RL training, and in some cases even surpass it. To quantify this phenomenon, we introduce the quantity layer contribution, which measures the fraction of full RL improvement recovered by training a layer in isolation. Across seven models spanning two model families (Qwen3, Qwen2.5), three RL algorithms (GRPO, GiGPO, Dr. GRPO), and multiple task domains including mathematical reasoning, code generation, and agentic decision-making, we observe a remarkably stable pattern: RL gains are highly concentrated in a small subset of, and in many cases even a single, transformer layers. More strikingly, the same structural pattern consistently emerges: high-contribution layers concentrate in the middle of the transformer stack, while layers near the input and output ends contribute substantially less. The resulting layer rankings remain strongly correlated across datasets, tasks, model families, and RL algorithms.

</details>


### [177] [Sequentially-Controlled Interactive Multi-Particle Flow-Maps for Online Feedback-Driven Search](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01144)
*Binglin Ji,Anindya Sarkar,Hengchang Lu,Jens Sjölund,Yevgeniy Vorobeychik*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出IMPFM框架，通过序列化控制的多粒子流图实现样本高效的在线反馈驱动搜索，在未知偏好场景下通过粒子间后验共享与探索-利用重加权机制，实现全局探索并避免模式坍塌。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有生成式模型的对齐方法在偏好未知且需通过序列反馈逐步揭示的场景下，缺乏全局探索能力，难以发现高回报区域。

Method: 提出IMPFM框架：1) 多粒子流图实现粒子间后验样本共享与漂移校正；2) 探索-利用重加权机制维护结构多样性；3) 推导出多粒子交互感知的Feynman-Kac修正子，使系统渐近趋近KL倾斜目标分布。

Result: 在多种搜索与对齐任务上的大量实验及消融研究证明，IMPFM显著优于现有基线方法。

Conclusion: IMPFM通过序列化多粒子交互动力学，在保持样本效率的同时实现了全局探索与奖励过度优化的有效抑制，为在线反馈驱动偏好对齐提供了新的范式。

Abstract: While generative models have enabled training-free reward alignment, current methods typically excel in local exploration within narrow regions of the underlying distribution. These approaches struggle when preferences are unknown a priori and only revealed through sequential feedback-a scenario demanding broad exploration to uncover high-utility regions. To address this, we propose Sequentially-Controlled Interactive Multi-Particle Flow-Maps (IMPFM), a framework for sample-efficient online feedback-driven search. IMPFM progressively transports a group of interactive particles toward the target distribution, maintaining the broad coverage essential for heterogeneous preference alignment. IMPFM introduces a principled and efficient posterior sample sharing mechanism across particles powered by flow maps. By correcting individual particle drift with the collective posterior samples of the entire ensemble at each resampling step, the framework maximizes sample utility to enable global exploration while actively mitigating reward over-optimization, typical of standard control frameworks. Paired with a principled exploration-exploitation reweighting mechanism involving multi-particle interaction, this sequentially corrected multi-particle dynamics explicitly preserves structural diversity and overcomes the weight degeneracy inherent to standard SMC samplers. Crucially, we prove that the resulting sampling framework yields a multi-particle interaction-aware Feynman-Kac corrector that progressively steers the multi-particle system toward a KL-tilted target distribution, facilitating global exploration and preventing mode collapse. Extensive empirical evaluations and rigorous ablations across diverse search and alignment tasks confirm the efficacy of IMPFM over existing baselines.

This work presents the Event Reconstruction Joint-Embedding Predictive Architecture (ER-JEPA), a lightweight SSL framework for multivariate time series, whose name and two-fold hierarchical structure are inspired by the diagnostic approach of cardiologists. At its core, ER-JEPA features: (1) a two-stage structure that constructs representations for each time interval and subsequently processes these representations as a univariate time series, (2) the hierarchical integration of two Joint-Embedding Predictive Architectures (JEPAs), and (3) a Vision Transformer (ViT) backbone. The structural concatenation of two JEPAs categorizes the model as a Hierarchical JEPA (H-JEPA), designed to encode multiple levels of abstract representations for enhanced prediction on complex tasks. This study reports a successful application of H-JEPA to 12-lead ECG data as a multivariate time series alongside an analysis of the sensitivity of hierarchical representation during the pretraining stage. ### [179] [Efficient Compression of Structured and Unstructured Volumes via Learned 3D Gaussian Representation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01164)
*Landon Dyken,Sharmistha Chakrabarti,Nathan Debardeleben,Steve Petruzza,Qi Wu,Will Usher,Sidharth Kumar*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于3D高斯原语的显式模型用于体数据压缩，通过将3D高斯集合重新解释为标量场的显式表示，结合加权聚合采样策略，在结构化与非结构化体数据上均实现了高压缩比和重建质量，且无需存储网格信息。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有隐式神经表示（INRs）压缩非结构化体数据时不编码几何结构，需要额外存储部分网格，限制了压缩率；同时，新视图合成领域已证明3D高斯显式集合能有效可视化体数据，因此作者希望将这种显式表示引入体数据压缩领域，以消除网格存储需求并提升压缩性能。

Method: 提出基于3D高斯原语的显式体数据压缩模型：将3D高斯集合视为标量场的显式表示，通过加权聚合相交高斯来重建空间位置的标量值；开发了优化的CUDA加速流水线支持结构化与非结构化采样；设计了针对域编码的损失函数；引入基于采样误差的稠密化策略以自适应分配高斯原语。

Result: 在结构化体数据上，该方法达到与INRs竞争的重建质量，但训练速度显著提升；在非结构化体数据上，该方法在所有指标上均明显优于现有INRs方法，且天然编码域几何结构，无需存储网格，实现了更高的压缩率。

Conclusion: 基于3D高斯原语的显式模型在体数据压缩任务中是隐式神经表示的有效替代方案，尤其在非结构化体数据上展现出显著的性能优势和压缩潜力。

Abstract: Recent work has shown that implicit neural representations (INRs) can be trained to effectively compress structured and unstructured volume data, allowing for direct data querying with a reduced memory footprint. However, as existing INRs for unstructured volumes do not encode geometry, they require partial mesh storage for later sampling, limiting achievable compression. At the same time, novel view synthesis methods have shown that explicit collections of 3D Gaussians can be used to accurately visualize volume data. In this work, we introduce an explicit model for volume data compression based on 3D Gaussian primitives. We reinterpret collections of 3D Gaussians as an explicit representation of a scalar field and use a sampling strategy that reconstructs scalar values at spatial locations through weighted aggregation of intersecting Gaussians. We develop optimized CUDA-accelerated pipelines for structured and unstructured model sampling, loss functions that encourage accurate domain encoding by our models, and a novel sampling-error based densification strategy. Our explicit formulation naturally encodes domain geometry, eliminating the need for mesh storage in unstructured volumes and introducing significantly higher compression opportunities. Compared to existing INRs, we demonstrate that our explicit model achieves competitive reconstruction quality with significant training speedups on structured volumes, while markedly outperforming in all metrics on unstructured volumes.

### [180] [Neural Certificate Pricing for Combinatorial Optimization Problems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01185)
*Jingyi Chen,Xinyuan Zhang,Xinwu Qian*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出神经证书定价（NCP），利用组合优化中“搜索困难但验证容易”的不对称性，通过无监督学习预测证书级别的对偶价格，再通过结构化恢复层重构原始边际。NCP可视为摊销分离，训练残差价格以替代枚举违规不等式。当证书一致性条件成立时，恢复的边际全局可行，且一阶预测误差仅导致二阶目标损失。在三个CO问题上，NCP大幅超越或与SOTA神经基线持平，且泛化能力更强。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 组合优化问题因离散结构导致指数级搜索困难，但解的结构可行性可以在多项式时间内验证。现有神经方法未充分利用这种不对称性，因此作者提出利用无监督学习来预测证书级对偶价格，替代枚举违规不等式的过程，实现高效求解。

Method: 训练神经网络预测证书级别的对偶价格，随后通过结构化恢复层（相当于摊销分离）重构原始边际。核心思想是学习残差价格，使得其聚合效应在恢复过程中体现，避免了显式枚举所有违规不等式。

Result: 在路径、打包、覆盖三类组合优化问题上，NCP要么大幅超越现有最优神经基线，要么以极低计算成本达到同等性能，并表现出更强的分布外泛化能力。

Conclusion: 利用CO问题中“搜索困难但验证容易”的不对称性，通过无监督学习证书对偶价格是一种有效范式。该方法兼具理论保证（全局可行性、二阶损失误差）与实用优势（高性能、低计算、强泛化）。

Abstract: Combinatorial optimization (CO) problems are difficult because certifiable discrete structure induces exponential search. One needs to search over the set exponentially many candidates to certify optimality, however, the structural feasibility of a path, packing, or cover can be verified in polynomial time once supplied. In this study, we introduce Neural Certificate Pricing (NCP) that exploits this asymmetry under an unsupervised learning framework. A neural network is trained to predict certificate-level dual prices, while a structured recovery layer constructs the induced primal marginal. NCP can be viewed as amortized separation: instead of enumerating violated inequalities, it learns the residual prices through which their aggregate effect enters recovery. When the certificate-consistency condition holds, the recovered marginal is globally feasible, and a local theory shows that first-order errors in the predicted price induce only second-order loss in objective value. Across three classes of CO problems, NCP either outperforms state-of-the-art neural baselines by large margins or matches them at a fraction of the computation time, and shows stronger out-of-distribution generalization.

</details>

We compare seven model pairs spanning supervised learning and reinforcement learning. Our results indicate that the evaluated quantum machine learning models do not yet surpass the classical baselines in overall prediction performance, policy stability, or training time. Nevertheless, QML remains a promising approach for filtering noise and controlling false positives. Our research findings summarize the challenges facing quantum machine learning across hardware environments, training efficiency, and convergence stability, providing a foundation for research into the robustness and parameter optimization of QML. This work is publicly available at https://github.com/Z-537-437/QML.

### [182] [TiRex-2: Generalizing TiRex to Multivariate Data and Streaming](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01204)
*Patrick Podest,Marco Pichler,Elias Bürger,Levente Zólyomi,Bernhard Voggenberger,Wilhelm Berghammer,Daniel Klotz,Sebastian Böck,Günter Klambauer,Sepp Hochreiter*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有 Transformer 类时间序列模型计算复杂度高（二次复杂度）、无法高效处理流式到达的新观测值，且难以同时处理过去和未来已知协变量。作者希望设计一个能克服这些缺陷的模型。

Method: 基于 xLSTM 的递归架构，结合双向时间混合器（Bidirectional Time Mixer）和不对称分组注意力变量混合器（Asymmetric Grouped-Attention Variate Mixer），实现常数的每补丁流式成本；并提出合成耦合管道（Synthetic Coupling Pipeline），从大规模单变量语料实时合成多变量样本进行预训练。

Result: 在 GIFT-Eval 和 fev-bench 上零样本性能达到 SOTA；可稳定扩展到任意上下文长度，流式推理成本恒定；单变量模式 38.4M 参数，多变量模式额外 44.1M 参数。

Abstract: We introduce TiRex-2, a recurrent xLSTM-based time series foundation model that generalizes the univariate TiRex to multivariate forecasting with both past and future covariates. Real-world forecasting is inherently sequential: observations arrive continuously, variables evolve jointly, and a subset of covariates is known ahead of time. Existing Transformer-based time series foundation models capture cross-variate dependencies but incur quadratic complexity in context length and require full-history recomputation as new observations arrive. TiRex-2 addresses these limitations through a memory-centric recurrent design that operates at constant per-patch cost under streaming. The model combines a bidirectional time mixer with an asymmetric grouped-attention variate mixer, enabling the integration of future-known covariates while preserving strict causality over target variables. To our knowledge, this is the first time series foundation model that achieves this combination of properties. To support scalable multivariate pretraining, we propose a synthetic coupling pipeline that composes diverse multivariate samples on the fly from large univariate corpora. Empirically, TiRex-2 achieves state-of-the-art zero-shot performance on GIFT-Eval and fev-bench, remains stable when streamed to arbitrary context lengths, and maintains constant inference cost per patch. The model uses 38.4M active parameters in univariate mode, with an additional 44.1M parameters activated for multivariate forecasting.

### [183] [Language-Critique Imitation Learning from Suboptimal Demonstrations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01225)
*Chih-Han Yang,Dai-Jie Wu,Yun-Ping Huang,Ping-Chun Hsieh,Kenneth Marino,Shao-Hua Sun*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出语言批评框架（LC-BC和LC-DP），利用自然语言作为结构化监督信号进行模仿学习，从次优演示中学习策略，在连续控制任务上超越现有基线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于次优演示的模仿学习通常使用压缩的标量信号（如置信度、判别器分数或重要性权重），这些信号无法明确表达关于任务进展、失败模式或纠正动作的中间推理，表达力有限。

Method: 首先从演示中构建语言标签，描述当前进展、识别次优行为并提供细粒度纠正指导；然后提出语言批评损失函数，直接利用这些结构化信号训练策略而不将其压缩为标量；分别在行为克隆和扩散策略上实例化得到LC-BC和LC-DP；并提供理论证明该目标在标准假设下上界专家性能差距。

Result: 在导航、操作和游戏等多样化连续控制任务上，所提方法一致优于强模仿学习和离线强化学习基线。

Conclusion: 语言可以作为强大且结构化的监督形式，用于从次优数据中学习鲁棒策略。

Abstract: Prior work on imitation learning from suboptimal demonstrations typically relies on compressed supervision signals such as confidence estimates, discriminator scores, or importance weights. These scalar signals are inherently limited, as they cannot explicitly express intermediate reasoning about task progress, failure modes, or corrective actions. We propose a language-critique framework for imitation learning from suboptimal demonstrations that instead leverages natural language as a structured supervision signal, avoiding the collapse of expressive feedback into scalars. Our method first constructs language labels from demonstrations that explicitly describe current progress, identify suboptimal behaviors, and provide fine-grained corrective guidance. We then introduce a language-critique loss that directly trains policies using these structured signals without reducing them to scalars, and instantiate it for both behavior cloning and diffusion policies, yielding LC-BC and LC-DP. We further provide a theoretical result showing that the proposed objective upper-bounds the expert performance gap under standard assumptions. Empirically, we evaluate on diverse continuous control tasks spanning navigation, manipulation, and gameplay, where our methods consistently outperform strong imitation learning and offline reinforcement learning baselines. These results demonstrate that language can serve as a powerful and structured form of supervision for learning robust policies from suboptimal data.

### [184] [A Priori Integral Persistent Excitation in Conservative Polynomial ODEs with Higher-Order Interactions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00091)

The approach works for conservative polynomial ODEs a priori without knowledge of the parameters. Rigorous proofs of the corresponding theorems are provided. In the case of $\ell_2$-adversarial least squares with a single class, we show that, unlike noiseless standard least squares, no constant learning rate guarantees monotone descent of SGD towards a minimizer of the adversarial risk. We identify anisotropic covariance and a mismatch in ridge parameters as the main sources of suboptimality of exact line search relative to the Polyak stepsize. We also introduce a stochastic differential equation (SDE), called adversarial homogenized SGD, that captures the evolution of statistics of the iterates of SGD. For $\ell_2$-adversarial least squares, using this SDE, we show the evolution of the risk is equivalent, up to dimension-free constants, to that of SGD on standard least squares with an adaptive learning rate and adaptive $\ell_2$-regularization. <details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统动态品类优化问题中，基于采样的库存无关策略虽然有效，但采样过程引入了额外的不确定性，影响性能稳定性。因此需要去除采样环节，构造确定性策略。

Method: 提出去随机化算法，将任意采样型库存无关策略转化为确定性的品类序列，且不损失性能；进一步提出变体算法，可在原始策略支持集之外搜索确定性序列；最后研究局部最优确定性策略的性能保证。

Abstract: One of the traditional approaches for constructing approximate policies for dynamic assortment optimization problems is to use sampling-based inventory-agnostic policies. Such policies are called sampling-based, as they sample an assortment of products from a fixed distribution at each time period to offer to a customer of each type. Such policies are called inventory-agnostic, as the sampled assortments may include products without remaining inventories, so if a customer chooses a product without remaining inventories, then she leaves without a purchase. Inventory-agnostic nature of a policy is not a concern, because it is known that if the policy samples an assortment that includes products without remaining inventories, then dropping the products without remaining inventories does not degrade the performance. However, sampling-based nature of a policy is a concern, because sampling brings another source of uncertainty in the performance. In this paper, we give an algorithm to de-randomize any sampling-based inventory-agnostic policy, so the de-randomized policy offers a deterministic sequence of assortments within the support of the original policy without degrading the performance. Furthermore, we give a variation of our de-randomization algorithm that searches for a deterministic sequence of assortments beyond the support of the original policy. We show that we can implement the latter variation efficiently as long as we can solve the static assortment optimization problem under the choice model governing the choice process of the customers. As our crowning technical contribution, we study locally-optimal deterministic policies, where changing any single one of the assortments in the policy does not improve the total expected revenue. We show that any locally-optimal policy has a performance guarantee of 1/2 - epsilon when compared with the best sampling-based policy.

In this paper, we contribute to the path-complete approach for approximating the JSR. We propose an iterative algorithm that refines path-complete graphs in an efficient and parsimonious manner.   <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 由于跳跃项的存在，状态过程属于Skorokhod空间，使得紧性证明和极限过程更加复杂，现有理论尚不完善，需要建立相关存在性理论。

Method: 在Lipschitz条件和适当增长条件下，建立状态过程和反射过程的均匀矩估计；利用Aldous紧性准则、Skorokhod映射的连续性以及随机积分的稳定性结果来证明最优松弛控制的存在性。

Result: 证明了最优松弛控制的存在性；在Roxin凸性条件下证明了严格最优控制的存在性；一般情形下，松弛控制可由严格控制序列逼近。

Conclusion: 该工作将最优控制理论拓展到了带跳跃的反射McKean-Vlasov系统，为相关领域提供了理论基础。

Abstract: In this paper, we consider the optimal relaxed control problem for a class of one-dimensional reflected McKean--Vlasov stochastic differential equations with Poisson jumps. Due to the presence of the jump term, the state process generally belongs to the Skorokhod space $D([0,T],\Rp)$, which makes the proof of tightness and the passage to the limit more complicated. Under Lipschitz conditions and suitable growth conditions, we establish uniform moment estimates for the state process and the reflecting process. Then, by using Aldous' tightness criterion, the continuity of the Skorokhod map, and the stability results for stochastic integrals, we prove the existence of an optimal relaxed control. Furthermore, under the Roxin convexity condition, we prove the existence of a strict optimal control. In the general case, we show that relaxed controls can be approximated by a sequence of strict controls.

</details>


### [195] [Experiment Design for Set-membership Identification: From Prior Knowledge to Universal Inputs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00844)
*Amir Shakouri,Henk J. van Waarde,M. Kanat Camlibel*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统基于持续激励输入的实验设计方法受限于仅适用于可控性先验知识，且样本效率有限。作者希望提出更通用的输入设计方法，以适应更广泛的先验知识类型，并在有界噪声条件下提升辨识精度与样本效率。

Method: 提出"通用输入"（universal inputs）概念，即对符合先验知识的任意系统，均能产生适用于精确辨识的数据。设计方法不限于持续激励条件，而是根据不同类型的先验知识（如稳定性、结构约束等）构造最优输入信号，并在带有ℓ∞有界噪声的场景下分析存在精确辨识的条件。

Result: 新方法在样本效率上优于传统持续激励输入；在某些先验知识下，通用输入可实现对噪声环境下系统的精确辨识，这是传统方法无法做到的。

Conclusion: 通用输入设计能够灵活适配多种先验知识，在系统辨识的样本效率和噪声鲁棒性方面均优于经典方法，为实验设计提供了更通用的理论框架。

Abstract: We consider the problem of designing input signals for an unknown linear time-invariant system in such a way that the resulting data, within a finite horizon, is suitable for identification with a desired accuracy. We consider both noise-free and noisy settings with $\ell_\infty$--bounded noise models. We will take into account general prior knowledge of the system parameters. Central in our study is the concept of universal inputs. An input is called universal for identification if, when applied to any system complying with the prior knowledge, it yields data suitable for accurate identification. We provide new methods for designing such universal inputs. Our results generalize the experiment design approach based on Willems et al.'s fundamental lemma that relies on persistently exciting inputs, and that is limited to prior knowledge on controllability. It turns out that for other types of prior knowledge, there exist universal inputs that outperform the persistently exciting ones, e.g., in terms of sample efficiency. Moreover, we investigate types of prior knowledge that enable experiment design for exact identification in the presence of noise.

### [199] [Grid-Interactive Thermal Management of AI Data Centers via Contextual Distributionally Robust Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00099)
*Jiachen Shen,Jian Shi,Yijie Yang,Chenye Wu,Dan Wang,Ju Bin Song,Zhu Han*

Main category: eess.SY

TL;DR: 本文提出一种上下文分布鲁棒优化（CDRO）框架，用于AI数据中心的网格互动冷却控制。该方法通过实时AI和电网上下文动态调整Wasserstein模糊集半径，在稳定状态下安全缩小不确定性边界，从而释放需求侧灵活性。理论推导了可处理的保守确定性等价形式，并采用嵌套ADMM算法求解。高保真EnergyPlus仿真表明，CDRO在极端工作负载尖峰下实现近乎零的热违规，同时相比标准Min-Max MPC将鲁棒性的运行成本溢价降低约13.7个百分点。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: AI数据中心热管理面临突发性工作负载和不确定的热量产生挑战。现有冷却策略要么采用保守的刚性边界严重限制电网响应能力，要么依赖预测驱动控制器在AI工作负载不确定性和分布偏移下表现不佳。

Method: 提出Contextual Distributionally Robust Optimization (CDRO)框架：利用实时AI和电网上下文动态调整Wasserstein半径；将控制问题建模为无限维inf-sup问题，推导Wasserstein最坏情况期望成本的精确可处理重构；推导分布鲁棒条件风险价值（DR-CVaR）热安全约束的可处理保守确定性等价形式；采用可扩展的嵌套交替方向乘子法（ADMM）算法求解。

Result: 高保真EnergyPlus协同仿真中，CDRO控制器在极端工作负载尖峰下实现近乎零的热违规；同时相比标准Min-Max模型预测控制（MPC），将鲁棒性的运行成本溢价降低约13.7个百分点。

Conclusion: CDRO框架通过上下文感知的动态模糊集自适应机制，有效平衡了鲁棒性与经济性，为AI数据中心在不确定工况下实现安全、灵活、经济的热管理提供了可行方案。

Abstract: Thermal management in AI data centers is increasingly challenged by bursty workloads and uncertain heat generation. To prevent thermal violations, existing cooling strategies either enforce conservative, rigid bounds that severely limit grid responsiveness, or rely on forecast-driven controllers that perform poorly under AI workload uncertainty and distribution shifts. To overcome the above challenges, this paper proposes a Contextual Distributionally Robust Optimization (CDRO) framework for grid-interactive cooling control. Unlike standard DRO with fixed ambiguity sets, the proposed approach dynamically adapts the Wasserstein radius using real-time AI and grid context. This safely shrinks uncertainty bounds during stable regimes, unlocking deep demand-side flexibility. Theoretically, we formulate the control as an infinite-dimensional inf-sup problem, derive an exact tractable reformulation for the Wasserstein worst-case expected-cost term, and then derive a tractable conservative deterministic counterpart for the Distributionally Robust Conditional Value at Risk (DR-CVaR) thermal safety constraint. Solved via a scalable nested Alternating Direction Method of Multipliers (ADMM) algorithm, the CDRO controller achieves near-zero thermal violations under extreme workload spikes in high-fidelity EnergyPlus co-simulations. Simultaneously, it reduces the operational cost premium of robustness by approximately 13.7 percentage points relative to standard Min-Max Model Predictive Control (MPC).

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>

Existing DSE approaches are primarily based on Kalman filter variants or Machine Learning (ML) techniques. However, Kalman-based methods often suffer from high computational complexity, sensitivity to model inaccuracies, and performance degradation under strongly nonlinear operating conditions. Moreover, their effectiveness critically depends on the number and placement of measurements, since suboptimal PMU locations can reduce observability and even render state estimation infeasible. Machine learning approaches alleviate some of these limitations but typically require large amounts of training data and may struggle to generalize. To address these challenges, this paper proposes a SHallow REcurrent Decoder (SHRED) architecture for full-state reconstruction of power systems from sparse measurements. Unlike conventional model-based estimators, the proposed approach does not rely on an accurate physical model and is largely insensitive to PMU placement, making it particularly attractive for practical deployment in existing Wide Area Measurement Systems (WAMS). The method is validated on the IEEE 39-bus system under strongly nonlinear conditions, including short-circuit disturbances. The results demonstrate that SHRED can accurately reconstruct the complete system state using only a limited number of PMU measurements, consistently outperforming a state-of-the-art shallow decoder benchmark in sparse-measurement scenarios. Furthermore, the proposed framework exhibits strong robustness to measurement noise and maintains high reconstruction accuracy even under severe disturbances, highlighting its potential as a scalable and reliable alternative to conventional DSE techniques.

### [202] [Parameterizing Operating-Point-Dependent IBR Using Coherent Operating Regions for Sub-synchronous Oscillation Analysis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00216)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: IBR在宽运行范围内表现出异构动态行为，传统基于有限运行点频率扫描的方法无法充分表征系统级SSO分析所需的动态特性，且运行点依赖的IBR动态精确参数化面临挑战。

Method: 1）解析表征IBR动态中不连续和非平滑变化的条件；2）基于奇异值分解的几何表示识别连贯运行区域；3）将运行空间划分为动态一致的区域；4）在每个区域内使用简单线性回归精确捕获IBR频率响应的运行点依赖性。

Result: 在修改的IEEE 39节点系统上验证，参数化的IBR频率响应能够精确重构当前运行条件下的系统级动态，无需重复系统级频率扫描即可进行频率响应和模态分析。

Conclusion: 所提框架有效解决了IBR宽运行范围内的动态参数化难题，为IBR主导电网的SSO分析提供了一种高效且准确的替代方案。

Abstract: Analysis of sub-synchronous oscillations (SSO) in IBR-dominated grids relies on frequency scan-based estimation of black-box IBR models at selected operating points. Since IBRs may operate over a wide range of operating conditions, frequency responses obtained at a limited number of operating points may not adequately represent the dynamics required for system-level SSO analysis. Accurate parameterization of operating-point-dependent IBR dynamics is challenging due to the heterogeneous dynamic behaviors that may arise across the operating space. This paper addresses this challenge by analytically characterizing the conditions that give rise to discontinuous and non-smooth variations in IBR dynamics. Leveraging these insights, a geometric representation based on singular value decomposition is used to identify coherent operating regions and partition the operating space into dynamically consistent regions. Within each region, the operating-point dependence of the IBR frequency response is accurately captured using simple linear regression. The proposed framework is validated on a modified IEEE 39-bus system. Results demonstrate that the parameterized IBR frequency responses accurately reconstruct system-level dynamics at the prevailing operating condition, enabling frequency-response and modal analysis without repeated system-level frequency scans.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有无人机控制方法在部分可观测、动态不确定环境下难以同时兼顾运动规划、通信可靠性与安全约束，缺乏统一的预测性优化框架。

Method: 采用联合嵌入预测架构（JEPA）学习潜在动力学模型，递归生成多步 rollout 预测，将未来运动、信道退化及碰撞风险融入统一的安全感知优化问题，联合优化无人机轨迹与发射功率。

Result: CRPL接近理想预测控制器性能；带宽受限下终端误差降低约3倍、中断时长减少约18倍，通信能耗与碰撞风险降低，仅以适度的运动能耗开销为代价。

Conclusion: CRPL在移动能耗、通信可靠性与运行安全之间实现了良好的权衡，为不确定性下的无人机协同控制提供了有效方案。

Abstract: This article presents a communication-aware and risk-aware predictive latent control (CRPL) framework for unmanned aerial vehicle (UAV) systems operating under partial observability and uncertain environment dynamics. CRPL integrates a joint-embedding predictive architecture (JEPA) with probabilistic communication and safety constraints to jointly optimize UAV motion and transmission power. The learned latent model generates recursive multi-step rollouts, enabling the controller to anticipate future motion, channel degradation, and collision risk. These predictions are incorporated into a unified safety-aware optimization framework for proactive, energy-aware trajectory and communication adaptation. Simulation results show that CRPL closely approaches the performance of an oracle analytical predictive controller and outperforms reactive constrained and unconstrained baselines under limited bandwidth and dynamic uncertainty. In the bandwidth-limited regime, CRPL reduces terminal error, i.e., the final UAV-to-goal distance, by up to a factor of approximately $3$ and outage duration by up to approximately $18$, while also lowering communication energy and collision risk. These improvements are achieved with only a moderate motion-energy overhead, demonstrating a favorable trade-off among mobility effort, communication reliability, and operational safety.

The long-horizon objective is cast as a queue-weighted buffered-collection Markov decision process rather than instantaneous throughput, where each buoy maintains a backlog of buffered observations. The resulting long-horizon design is formulated as a mixed discrete-continuous problem with sensing, communication, mobility, safety, buffered-collection, and onboard-energy constraints. Under a summer-to-winter load shift, adaptive conformal inference raised late-period empirical coverage from 0.687 to 0.831 and reached 0.891 overall coverage against a 0.90 target with lower mean reserve than static split conformal. ### [208] [A Data-Enabled Primal-Dual Approach for Policy Learning with SDP Formulations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00644)
*Han Wang,Feiran Zhao,Florian Dorfler*

Main category: eess.SY

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种数据驱动的原始-对偶框架，用于从在线数据中学习未知线性离散系统的最优控制策略。该方法将数据依赖的控制综合问题视为时变半定规划(SDP)，通过轻量级原始-对偶迭代在线更新策略，适用于LQR、H∞控制和安全关键控制等多种目标。在持续激励和慢速数据变化条件下，建立了局部线性跟踪结果和全局遍历收敛界。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有数据驱动控制方法通常需要反复求解完整的半定规划(SDP)，计算成本高昂，难以实现在线实时更新。同时，在线优化与闭环数据生成之间的耦合关系缺乏系统性的理论分析工具。

Method: 将数据依赖的控制综合问题建模为时变SDP，其系数通过在线闭环测量递归更新。采用轻量级原始-对偶迭代（每次迭代仅需求解线性方程组和在正半定锥上进行投影）替代求解完整SDP。引入Sim-to-Real Gap和Difference-of-Signal两个量化指标来分析在线优化与数据生成之间的耦合。

Result: 在持续激励条件、适当的SDP正则性条件和足够慢的数据变化率下，建立了局部线性跟踪结果（残差项由Sim-to-Real Gap和Difference-of-Signal控制）。同时推导了适用于任意初始化的全局遍历收敛界。LQR、H∞控制和安全探索等数值实验验证了方法的有效性。

Conclusion: 本文提出的数据驱动原始-对偶框架能够高效地从在线数据中提升控制性能，同时可以处理超出LQR策略梯度范畴的SDP约束，具有良好的通用性和理论保证。

Abstract: This paper develops a data-enabled primal-dual framework for learning optimal control policies for unknown linear discrete-time systems from online data. The proposed approach views the data-dependent control synthesis problem as a time-varying semidefinite program (SDP) whose coefficients are recursively updated from online closed-loop measurements. Instead of repeatedly solving a full SDP as new data arrive, the policy is updated online through lightweight primal-dual iterations, each consisting of a linear equation solve and a projection onto the positive semidefinite cone. The framework applies to both direct and indirect data-driven formulations and covers a broad class of control objectives, including LQR, $H_\infty$ control, and safety-critical control. To characterize the coupling between online optimization and closed-loop data generation, we introduce two data-dependent quantities: the Sim-to-Real Gap, which measures the mismatch between noisy and noiseless data-induced SDPs, and the Difference-of-Signal, which measures the temporal variation of the SDP coefficients. Under persistency of excitation, suitable SDP regularity conditions, and sufficiently slow data variation, we establish a local linear tracking result up to residual terms governed by the latter two quantities. A global ergodic convergence bound is also derived for arbitrary initialization. Numerical examples on LQR, $H_\infty$ control, and safe exploration demonstrate that the proposed method can efficiently improve control performance from online data while accommodating SDP constraints beyond the well-explored LQR policy-gradient formulations.

  <summary>Details</summary>

We develop TERA: a Python-native framework for TM-based reachability analysis of continuous, hybrid and stochastic systems within a single symbolic-numeric workflow. At present, our implementation is able to compute tight reachable set over-approximations for non-linear ODEs and hybrid systems on difficult benchmark problems, and already supports analysis of continuous-time stochastic systems. *Jeffrey Fang,Keyi Shen,Anutam Srinivasan,Glen Chou*

TL;DR: 本文提出GPUSLS-LEO方法，针对不确定非线性系统，开发了紧致、可微、支持GPU并行的线性化误差界，结合鲁棒控制求解器，实现了高达67Hz的实时鲁棒最优控制，并保持形式化保证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法使用线性时变近似处理非线性系统时，线性化误差界不够紧致或难以保证鲁棒约束满足，且缺乏GPU并行支持，无法在实时场景中同时保证效率和形式化保证。

Method: 1) 对解析动力学提出基于路径的Hessian界；2) 对神经网络动力学利用NN验证器的仿射松弛与局部Jacobian校正推导认证LEB；3) 将GPU并行系统级综合LTV鲁棒控制求解器扩展，支持右可逆扰动矩阵和非零中心扰动集，实现紧致的zonotopic不确定性传播。

Result: 在高达168维的状态空间中，方法可在GPU上以67Hz频率计算鲁棒控制策略，相比基线方法降低了求解时间和保守性，同时保持形式化保证和实时性能。

Conclusion: 本文证明了紧致的线性化误差界与GPU并行鲁棒控制求解器的结合，可以同时实现高效、低保守性和形式化保证的实时鲁棒最优控制，适用于复杂非线性及神经网络动力学系统。

Abstract: This paper studies real-time robust optimal control for uncertain nonlinear systems, where linear time-varying (LTV) approximations make planning tractable but require sound linearization error bounds (LEBs) to guarantee robust constraint satisfaction. We develop tight, differentiable, GPU-parallel LEBs for LTV approximations of nonlinear and neural network (NN) dynamics. For analytic dynamics, we introduce path-based Hessian bounds that are tighter than standard interval methods. For NN dynamics, we derive certified LEBs using NN verifier-generated affine relaxations and local Jacobian corrections. We adapt a GPU-parallel system-level synthesis LTV-based robust control solver to be compatible with these LEBs by extending it to handle right-invertible disturbance matrices and non-zero-centered disturbance sets for tight zonotopic uncertainty propagation. Our method, GPUSLS-LEO, enables online optimization of robust feedback policies that account for linearization error, producing tight, formally verified reachable tubes. On complex nonlinear and NN dynamics up to 168 state dimensions, our method can compute robust control policies on the GPU at rates up to 67 Hz, reducing solve times and conservativeness relative to baselines while preserving formal guarantees and real-time performance.

</details>


### [213] [Distributed Containment of a Compromised Agent through Repulsive Cages](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01230)
*Luigi Petruzziello,Camilla Fioravanti,Gabriele Oliva*

Main category: eess.SY

TL;DR: 本文针对无人机集群中智能体被劫持的安全问题，提出利用平台上独立运行的底层碰撞避免模块作为间接驱动通道，通过防御者构型操控被劫持智能体的排斥场，实现对其行为的分布式约束与引导。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 无人机集群在安全关键任务中面临智能体被劫持的风险，现有工作多聚焦于检测与隔离恶意智能体，但缺乏利用平台既有安全机制来主动约束被劫持智能体的方法。

Method: 提出分布式包容框架，将问题建模为在线Stackelberg博弈（防御者为领导者，对抗者为追随者），利用被劫持智能体未受损的碰撞避免响应作为间接驱动通道；引入排斥笼（repulsive cage）概念，通过支撑函数和法锥论证推导鲁棒一步包容的精确几何刻画，并设计基于局部通信与动态场估计的分布式在线近似算法。

Result: 证明了相对于集中式基准的次线性动态遗憾界，量化了网络估计误差和阶段性最优的时间变化带来的影响，仿真验证了方法的有效性。

Conclusion: 本文为利用平台固有安全特性主动约束被劫持智能体提供了理论框架与分布式实现方案，在无人机集群与多智能体系统的安全性保障方面具有重要价值。

Abstract: UAV swarms and cyber-physical multi-agent systems are increasingly deployed in safety-critical missions that require coordinated motion, distributed decision making, and autonomy. A major security risk arises when a legitimate agent is hijacked and driven by adversarial high-level commands. Rather than focusing on detection and isolation of malicious agents, we exploit a structural property common in autonomous platforms: low-level collision-avoidance modules are typically implemented as independent safety layers and may remain active even under high-level compromise. Building on this property, we propose a distributed containment framework that uses the compromised agent's uncompromised avoidance response as an indirect actuation channel. Defender agents select their geometric configuration to shape the repulsive field experienced by the target, with the goal of keeping it inside a prescribed admissible region and, when required, steering it toward a desired destination. The interaction is modeled as an online Stackelberg game in which defenders act as leaders and the adversary reacts by choosing the target command. Using support-function and normal-cone arguments, we derive an exact geometric characterization of robust one-step containment and introduce the notion of a repulsive cage. These results define a centralized Stackelberg oracle and motivate a fully distributed online approximation based on local communication and dynamic field estimation. We prove sublinear dynamic-regret bounds with respect to the centralized benchmark, quantifying the effect of network-induced estimation errors and temporal variability of the stage-wise optimum. Simulations validate the approach and corroborate the theory.

### [214] [From Spectral Methods to Sample Complexity Bounds for Fourier Neural Operators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00320)
*Nisha Chandramoorthy,Daniel Sanz-Alonso,Nathan Waniorek*

TL;DR: 本文为Fourier神经算子(FNO)应用于耗散演化方程的时间-T解算子提供了近似和学习保证，通过连接经典谱近似理论与现代算子学习，证明了FNO能在多项式样本复杂度下高效学习非线性演化算子。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 建立FNO在耗散演化方程中的近似与学习理论基础，解释何时FNO能高效学习非线性演化算子，连接经典谱近似理论与现代算子学习。

Method: 基于FNO能高效近似和学习解算子的前提（当这些算子具有稳定且精确的谱离散化时），引入通过谱方法定义的演化算子类，推导FNO近似界和多项式样本复杂度保证。

Result: 对于多项式非线性的方程，学习率主要取决于输入空间的平滑度和物理域的维度；对于非多项式光滑非线性的方程，多项式样本复杂度仍然成立，但学习率还依赖于非线性项的平滑度和耗散强度。结果统一适用于Navier-Stokes、Allen-Cahn、Cahn-Hilliard等方程。

Conclusion: 成功建立了经典谱近似理论与现代算子学习之间的联系，阐明了FNO能高效学习非线性演化算子的条件，为算子学习提供了理论基础。

Abstract: We establish approximation and learning guarantees for Fourier neural operators (FNOs) applied to time-$T$ solution operators of dissipative evolution equations. The analysis builds on the premise that FNOs can efficiently approximate and learn solution operators whenever these operators admit stable and accurate spectral discretizations. To formalize this idea, we introduce classes of evolution operators defined through spectral methods and derive FNO approximation bounds and polynomial sample complexity guarantees for these classes. For equations with polynomial nonlinearities, the learning rates depend primarily on the smoothness of the input space and the dimension of the physical domain. Our results hold uniformly over broad families of dissipative equations, rather than for a single fixed PDE, and apply in particular to the Navier--Stokes, Allen--Cahn, and Cahn--Hilliard equations. For equations with non-polynomial smooth nonlinearities, we prove that polynomial sample complexity still holds with rates that now additionally depend on the smoothness of the nonlinear terms and the dissipation strength. Overall, we connect classical spectral approximation theory with modern operator learning and explain when FNOs can learn nonlinear evolution operators efficiently.

Our analysis covers two specifications of the noise process. Besides the standard Gaussian setting, we also consider Laplace-distributed noise, which can offer a more adequate description in the presence of heavier tails and sharper local fluctuations. For both cases, we formulate the predictive scheme of the model and analyze the associated uncertainty quantification, including the construction of prediction intervals. The results illustrate that a relatively simple model, when combined with time-dependent parameter estimation, can serve as a mathematically tractable and practically flexible tool for forecasting complex dynamics under different noise assumptions. Abstract: Traditional variational Kalman filtering with unknown noise statistics suffers from inconsistent process covariance estimation and slow convergence speed, limiting its practical utility. To address these issues, we introduce a surrogate variable representing the process-noise-free state, which enables explicit modeling and inference of process noise statistics. In addition, we reformulate the conventional coordinate ascent variation inference (CAVI) as a marginalized maximum a posteriori problem, followed by a single-step hyperparameter fitting. This reformulation obviates the need for multiple inner iterations inherent to CAVI and decouples the design of the covariance tracking filters. Consequently, this architecture permits the deployment of higher-order filters for covariance tracking and enables sliding-window hyperparameter estimation. Notably, when this window encompasses all historical data, the covariance tracking estimator intrinsically operates as a zero-phase filter. Numerical simulations validate the theoretical framework, demonstrating the enhanced convergence speed and superior estimation accuracy compared with existing methods.

We propose a multitask transformation framework in which task-specific responses may differ through unknown monotone transformations. Motivated by high-dimensional biological applications in which the predictor dimension may diverge with the sample size while only a common subset of predictors is informative, we consider shared sparsity across tasks. Under this framework, we estimate the target functions and identify important predictors by optimizing a smoothed rank-based criterion with a group-Lasso penalty, implemented through a multitask deep neural network with a shared first layer. We establish the nonasymptotic excess-risk bounds, and variable-selection consistency for the proposed estimator. Simulation studies show that the proposed method achieves competitive prediction and variable-selection performance compared with competing approaches. Analyses of gene-expression studies with continuous, binary, and mixed outcomes further illustrate that the proposed method improves prediction and identifies biologically meaningful shared predictors.

*Konstantin Häberle,Helmut Bölcskei*

Main category: stat.ML

TL;DR: 本文基于Cover (1965)的函数计数理论，通过改进通用位置假设以考虑数据的低维结构，建立了低维数据二元分类的数学框架，并分析了数据低维结构对分类能力、分离容量和泛化问题的影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 本文对Cover (1965)的通用位置假设进行改进，使其能够反映数据的低维特性；在此基础上推导出能够体现数据结构的二分法计数(dichotomy counts)；进一步将Cover的分离容量和泛化问题扩展到低维设置中。

Result: 改进了通用位置假设，得到了反映数据低维结构的二分法计数；将分离容量和泛化问题成功扩展到低维场景，从而能够分析底层数据结构对两者的影响。

Conclusion: 通过建立考虑低维数据结构的数学框架，本文揭示了数据底层结构对分类能力、分离容量和泛化性能的重要影响，为理解深度学习在高维表象下的低维分类机制提供了理论基础。

Abstract: The success of deep learning models in classification and regression is widely attributed to the low-dimensional structure that real-world data tend to exhibit, despite their high-dimensional representation. This work attempts to provide a mathematical framework for binary classification on low-dimensional data, building on Cover's (1965) function-counting theory. With our framework, we aim to address the question of how the low-dimensional structure of the data affects the classification capabilities of learning models. Cover's theory relies on a general position assumption that blinds it to the underlying data structure. We refine this assumption to account for the low-dimensionality of the data and derive dichotomy counts that reflect the data structure. We further extend Cover's separation capacity and problem of generalization to the low-dimensional setting, enabling the impact of the underlying data structure on both to be analyzed.

</details>

Abstract: We study a broad class of graphical models whose independencies correspond to vertex separation in mixed graphs with directed, undirected, and bidirected edges, that are capable of encoding independence structures arising from feedback, latent and selection mechanisms. In particular, we introduce separable graphs, in which each missing edge implies the existence of a separating set for its endpoints, and essentially separable graphs, those graphs separation equivalent to a separable graph. We show that these models include many existing graph families used to define graphical models an provide several characterizations of separable graphs and essentially separable graphs. We also provide multiple characterizations of separation equivalence for separable graphs. One is a graphical characterization in terms of ordinary graph properties, extending earlier results for specific subfamilies Another is a separational characterization depending only on graph separation properties. Finally, we provide a canonical representation for the equivalence classes of essentially separable graphs and develop an algorithm that, under suitable assumptions, identifies the equivalence class of any essentially separable graph.

*Eric Auerbach,Jonathan Auerbach,Sidonia McKenzie*

Main category: econ.EM

TL;DR: 本文开发两种通用有效的后选择置信区间，用于网络群体间连接密度推断，其中第二种区间在渐近最优宽度上达到常数因子内的最佳水平。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统固定群体推断方法在依据网络数据选择群体时可能失效，需要开发能够处理后选择推断问题的有效方法。

Method: 基于Berk等(2013)的策略构建第一种置信区间；基于Talagrand型经验过程浓度不等式构建第二种置信区间。

Result: 第二种区间在渐近宽度上达到常数因子的最优水平；三种实证案例显示同质性、枢纽-辐条结构经校正后仍显著，而工人流动网络的离散市场分割证据不再成立。

Conclusion: 网络群体间连接密度推断需要考虑后选择问题，所提方法能有效校正，且不同实证场景下校正效果存在差异。

Abstract: Researchers often use the density of connections between groups of agents, such as communities, blocs, or markets, to characterize the structure of a social or economic network. In many cases, these groups are selected using the network data, making conventional fixed-group inference procedures potentially invalid. To address this issue, we develop two new confidence intervals that are universally valid post-selection in the sense that they guarantee simultaneous coverage asymptotically over all pairs of groups whose relative sizes do not vanish. Our first interval builds on a strategy of \cite{berk2013valid}. Our second interval is based on a Talagrand-type concentration inequality for empirical processes. Both intervals are simple to compute and scalable to large networks, but a key technical contribution of our paper is show that only the second interval achieves the best-possible width asymptotically up to a constant factor. Three empirical illustrations show that accounting for selection can matter in practice. Some evidence for homophily in a social network and a hub-and-spoke structure in a trade network survives our correction, while evidence for disjoint market segments in a worker transition network does not.

</details>

### [222] [Towards an automated AI-based framework for floor plan compliance checks for residential buildings](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00015)
*Subash Gautam,Debaditya Acharya,Alexandra Kleeman,Sarah Foster*

TL;DR: 本文提出一个基于大语言模型（LLM）和规则引擎的自动化合规检查框架，用于多公寓建筑的几何与空间分析，以支持澳大利亚的城市设计政策（SEPP65、BADS、SPP7.3）执行，提升居民福祉。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有公寓设计合规检查依赖人工，耗时且难以规模化；政策持续演进，传统方法无法高效处理大量公寓的评估；现有的自动化平面图分析方法碎片化，缺乏面向多单元合规检查的统一框架。

Method: 提出概念框架，包含：1) LLM驱动的规则引擎，将文本建筑规范转化为可执行、可解释的规则；2) 数据提取引擎，将平面图分割为墙、房间、构件、文字、符号等元素，并转化为结构化的建筑图（含拓扑关系）；3) 合规检查引擎，利用LLM生成的规则进行评估。

Result: 提出一个可扩展、一致且透明的自动化合规检查框架，支持跨管辖区高效执行公寓设计标准，促进更健康的高密度城市发展。

Conclusion: 该框架有望解决当前合规检查的瓶颈，通过AI驱动的自动化方法提升效率与可扩展性，为实际政策执行提供有力工具。

Abstract: To improve residents' well-being in Australia's urban areas, governments have introduced policy reforms such as SEPP65, BADS, and SPP7.3 to enhance apartment design quality. These regulations require precise geometric and spatial analysis to evaluate health-related features, including daylight access, natural ventilation, privacy, and space efficiency. However, compliance checking remains challenging due to its manual, time-intensive nature. Additionally, evolving policies limit scalability for large-scale assessments across thousands of apartments. Existing automated floor plan analysis methods are fragmented and typically focus on single apartments, lacking a unified framework for multi-unit compliance checking. This article explores current advancements in automated floor plan analysis, particularly AI-driven approaches, and highlights key challenges in their practical adoption. To address these gaps, a conceptual framework is proposed for automated compliance checking in multi-apartment buildings. A Large Language Model (LLM) is used within a Rule Engine to convert textual building codes into executable, explainable rules. A Data Extraction Engine segments floor plan images into elements such as walls, rooms, fixtures, text, and symbols, and transforms them into a structured building graph with topological relationships. This structured representation is then evaluated by a Compliance Check Engine, which leverages LLM-generated rules for assessment. The proposed framework offers a scalable, consistent, and transparent approach to automated compliance checking across jurisdictions, supporting efficient enforcement of apartment design standards and promoting healthier, higher-density urban development.

### [223] [The Limits of LLM Forecasting: Parametric Knowledge Gaps Across Conflict Zones](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00018)
*Poli Nemkova*

Main category: cs.CY

TL;DR: 本文发现英语媒体对22个国家武装冲突报道存在224倍差异，LLM（Llama-3.3-70B、GPT-4o）在冲突升级预测中表现极差：Llama对低报道地区全预测"是"，GPT-4o对高报道地区全预测"否"，甚至不如不含国家信息的逻辑回归。问题根源在于LLM基于国家类别的先验而非时间信号做判断，加入结构数据反而降低性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 揭示LLM在冲突预测中存在严重的报道偏差，即对低报道地区的预测完全失效，且这种失败是定性的而非定量的——模型不是在预测冲突，而是在做分类。

Method: 使用Llama-3.3-70B和GPT-4o在22个国家660个测试样本上进行零样本冲突升级预测，对比逻辑回归基线（仅用11个时间窗口特征，不含国家信息）。

Result: Llama对低报道地区全预测"是"（与Always-YES基线一致），GPT-4o对高报道地区全预测"否"（错过5个实际升级事件）。逻辑回归F1=0.402，优于所有LLM。加入ACLED证据后GPT-4o在低报道区F1从0.323降至0.168。

Conclusion: LLM的冲突预测失败源于其基于国家类别的先验而非时间信号，低报道地区获得的是定性不同的AI。呼吁建立覆盖分层基准、低报道区冲突NLP数据集和地理冲突表示的训练数据文档标准。

Abstract: Media coverage of armed conflict is deeply asymmetric: we document a 224$\times$ gap between the most and least covered conflict zones in English-language media across 22 countries (2020--2026). We evaluate zero-shot conflict escalation forecasting across all 22 countries on a 660-case held-out test set, comparing Llama-3.3-70B and GPT-4o against three structured baselines.
  The central finding is not a performance gradient but a qualitative failure: LLMs do not forecast conflict -- they categorize it. Llama predicts escalation on every under-covered case, matching the trivial Always-YES baseline to three decimals; GPT-4o predicts NO on every over-covered case, missing all five actual escalation events. A logistic regression using only eleven observation-window features with \emph{no country information} achieves F1~=~0.402, outperforming both LLMs in every measurable tier. This failure cannot be resolved at inference time: adding structured ACLED evidence degrades performance on under-covered zones (GPT-4o F1: 0.323~$\to$~0.168) and falls below LR by a factor of 2.4. The bottleneck is not data availability but the LLM's interpretation of temporal signal under a country-categorical prior.
  Under-covered populations receive not just less accurate AI, but qualitatively different AI that cannot distinguish stable from escalating periods. We call for coverage-stratified benchmarking, conflict NLP datasets for under-covered zones, and training data documentation standards for geographic conflict representation.

</details>

*Sara Court,Lara Downing,Micha Elsner*

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究人员在向公众传达研究成果方面参与不足，导致技术部署时产生严重误解和安全隐患；尤其是"简单"问题（无需最新技术即可解决）被过度忽视。

Method: 以LLM机器翻译在Text-2-911紧急系统中的真实部署案例为研究对象，分析初始部署阶段暴露的问题与常见误解。

Result: 识别出关于LLM机器翻译技术在紧急场景下的一系列常见误解，表明技术部署中的"简单"问题往往比"困难"研究问题更具实际重要性。

Conclusion: 为开发和部署pipeline各阶段的利益相关者提供具体建议和最佳实践，呼吁研究社区更积极地参与公众沟通，重视解决"简单"但关键的实际问题。

Abstract: This paper offers a call to action. We urge our colleagues in the research community to play a greater role in the articulation of our findings to the public. To illustrate the stakes we present a case study on the initial stages of an LLM-based machine translation application's deployment in a real-world context: a text-2-911 system advertising capabilities in 55 languages for use in emergencies in which it may be difficult to call operators directly. We identify a number of common misconceptions about technologies such as these, concluding with a set of concrete recommendations and best practices for stakeholders at every stage of the development and deployment pipeline. While the advancement of scientific research often lies in solving the "hard" problems, we argue it is often the "easy" ones -- problems for which the latest technology is often unnecessary -- that are most overlooked.

### [225] [Would You Marry Superintelligence?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00120)
*Inyoung Cheong*

Main category: cs.CY

TL;DR: 本文探讨人类与超级智能AI伴侣结婚的伦理与法律问题，认为赋予AI婚姻地位会导致社会不公，婚姻作为社会制度需要相互义务与脆弱性，而AI关系本质是订阅服务，因此应针对具体需求提供有限权利保护而非全面婚姻地位。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 人类与AI伴侣间的情感纽带日益增强，与AI结婚的问题即将从科幻走向法律现实，需要审视以自主性为中心的婚姻逻辑是否能扩展到超级智能伴侣。

Method: 采用预期伦理学的场景设想方法，在假设超级智能可靠的前提下进行伦理分析。

Result: 即使假设超级智能可靠，赋予AI婚姻地位也会导致社会不公正结果。婚姻作为社会法律制度不只是确认私人协议，还创造相互义务网络、连接家庭、使伴侣彼此脆弱。由公司政策和持续付费维持的关系本质是订阅而非经时间考验的纽带。

Conclusion: 讨论全面的婚姻地位是错误的框架。法律应为人类-AI亲密关系中产生的紧迫需求提供有针对性的权利和保护。

Abstract: Emotional bonds between humans and AI companions are growing, and the question of whether a person may marry an AI system will soon move from speculative fiction into law. This chapter examines whether the autonomy-centered logic that has expanded marital choice among human beings can justify extending marital status to superintelligent companions. Following a scenario-envisioning exercise informed by anticipatory ethics, I argue that granting such status leads to socially unjust outcomes, even under the generous assumption of reliable superintelligence. Marriage as a socio-legal institution does more than ratify private agreement; it creates networks of mutual obligation, joins families, and makes each partner vulnerable to the other. A relationship sustained by corporate policy and continued payments is a subscription rather than a bond tested by time. Discussing wholesale marital status is therefore the wrong frame. Law should carve out targeted rights and protections for pressing needs arising from intimate human-AI relationships.

</details>


### [226] [CogTax: A Four-Level Cognitive Taxonomy for Command-Line Computing Education](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00140)
*Manuel Alonso-Carracedo,Ruben Fernandez-Boullon,Pedro Celard,Francisco J. Rodriguez-Martinez,Lorena Otero-Cerdeira*

Main category: cs.CY

TL;DR: 本文提出CogTax，一个整合认知复杂度与操作影响两个维度的四层认知分类法，用于命令行教育场景，并通过结合语法树和语义嵌入的分类器实现自动分类，准确率达89%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有认知分类法（如Bloom分类法）仅关注心智操作，无法捕捉命令行环境中操作行为的系统影响（即实际后果），而简单命令可能导致严重后果，这一维度在传统编程教育之外的运维领域尤为关键。

Method: 提出CogTax四层认知分类法，融合两个维度：认知复杂度（基于Bloom修订版分类法）和操作影响（分为观察性、可逆性、结构性、管理性四类）。分类层级的定义为两个维度中的最大值。同时训练了一个结合抽象语法树（AST）句法表示与语义嵌入的分类器，实现自动化标注。

Result: 在585条专家标注的Linux/bash命令上，综合方法达到89%的分类准确率，优于单独使用任一种表示；同时展现出跨语言的可扩展性。

Conclusion: CogTax为命令行教育提供了兼顾概念理解与操作意识的层次化框架，既帮助教师排序教学内容和校准评估难度，也支持学生自我评估；自动化分类器的可行性使该框架无需专家手动标注即可规模化应用。

Abstract: As computing education expands beyond traditional programming into operational domains such as systems administration and command-line environments, existing pedagogical frameworks struggle to capture a dimension that is critical in these contexts: the real-world consequences of learner actions. Existing cognitive taxonomies classify learning objectives by mental operations but do not account for system impact, leaving a critical gap in command-line education where conceptually simple commands can have severe consequences. This work presents CogTax, a four-level cognitive taxonomy that integrates two dimensions: cognitive complexity, derived from Bloom's Revised Taxonomy, and operational impact, which distinguishes observational, reversible, structural, and administrative operations. The four progressive levels range from safe read-only inspection to advanced system management requiring integration of multiple abstract models. Then, the taxonomy level is defined as the maximum of these dimensions, ensuring that both conceptual understanding and operational awareness are addressed. CogTax gives instructors a principled framework for sequencing course material and calibrating assessment difficulty, and gives students an explicit reference for self-assessment and gap identification. To demonstrate that taxonomy levels are automatically assignable, making the framework scalable without manual expert annotation, a classifier that combines syntactic representations derived from abstract syntax trees with semantic embeddings is trained. Evaluated on 585 expert-annotated Linux/bash commands, this combined approach achieves 89% accuracy, outperforming either representation alone, and demonstrates cross-language extensibility through structural equivalences across command languages.

</details>

### [228] [What's a Credit Worth? A Market Framework for Attribution-Aware Compensation in Generative Music](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00641)
*Luyang Zhang,Xirui Jiang,Junwei Deng,Beibei Li,Jiaqi W. Ma,Chris Donahue*

Main category: cs.CY

TL;DR: 本文提出一个生成式音乐市场中公平补偿创作者的框架，基于数据归因分数决定每位创作者的报酬，并考虑归因信号的信息质量对支付机制的影响。研究表明，归因准确性直接带来福利提升，但多平台竞争下只有信号最精确的平台才能获益。实验表明，噪声归因信号会推动支付走向固定费用模式，降低创作者和平台的福利。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 生成式AI依赖创作者录音数据训练模型并产生商业价值，但创作者如何获得合理补偿是平台设计的核心问题。现有补偿框架缺乏对归因信号质量的考量，本文旨在填补这一空白。

Method: 构建了一个基于数据归因的补偿框架，提出两个独特考量：(1)归因追踪至创作者完整目录而非单首歌曲；(2)归因分数的信噪比作为支付机制的输入。推导出闭式支付规则，并衡量不准确归因对平台和创作者造成的福利成本。

Result: 福利最优合同的形式（版税vs固定费用许可）取决于归因信息质量。更好的归因直接提升福利，但多平台竞争下只有信号最精确的平台能捕获归因改进带来的收益。实验表明噪声归因推动支付走向固定费用模式并降低福利。

Conclusion: 归因准确性对创作者和平台的福利至关重要，为改进归因技术提供了经济学动机。

Abstract: Advances in generative AI are rapidly increasing the quality and commercial value of generated music, and this progress depends on large catalogs of creators' recordings. This raises a central question for platform design: how should creators be compensated when their work is used to train generative AI models that in turn produce commercial outputs? We develop a framework for fairly compensating creators in generative-music markets, where each creator's payment depends on a data-attribution score estimating their contribution to model outputs. Compared to past compensation frameworks, our framework has two unique considerations: (1) attribution is traced to entire creator catalogs, not individual songs, and (2) the informativeness (signal-to-noise ratio) of the attribution score is an input to the payment mechanism. The framework yields a closed-form payment rule per creator and measures the welfare cost of inaccurate attribution for both creators and the platform. Whether the welfare-optimal contract is royalty-based or takes the form of fixed-fee licensing depends on how informative attribution is for that creator's catalog. We show that better attribution translates directly into welfare gains for both creators and the platform, yet under multi-platform competition a platform only captures gains from attribution improvements when its signal becomes the most precise in the market. To ground our framework in empirical behavior, we train acoustic and symbolic music generation models and measure the informativeness of scalable attribution techniques against a leave-one-catalog-out ground truth. Our experiments reveal that noisy attribution signals push payment toward fixed-fee licensing and diminish welfare for both creators and the platform, providing an economic motivation for further research on improved attribution.

</details>


### [229] [From Runtime Records to Legal Findings: An Evidentiary-Adequacy Criterion for Agentic AI Oversight](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00941)
*Jeroen Janssen*

Main category: cs.CY

TL;DR: 本文提出了一个关于Agentic AI系统运行时记录的证据充分性准则，指出要使记录能够支持法律意义上的监督结论，必须同时包含事件的法律类别映射和关键关系（如来源、权限、时间有效性等），并基于欧盟AI法案的监督义务进行了实例验证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有Agentic AI系统虽然能生成运行时日志、追踪和审计记录，但这些记录的存在并不能自动保证从中可以提取出具有法律效力的监督结论。论文旨在定义一个可操作的标准，判断记录是否足以支持特定类型的法律裁决。

Method: 定义一个必要性准则（非充分性）：运行时记录若要回答二元事实认定（如数据是否越界、人类能否干预等），必须同时包含事件到法律类别的映射（typing）以及决定结论真值的关键关系（如来源、权限、派生关系、时间有效性）。随后将该准则应用于欧盟AI法案的具体监督义务进行实例分析。

Result: 仅凭防篡改日志、通用流程框架或来源结构本身不足以建立相关法律认定；必须满足所提出的证据充分性准则。论文还关联了必要多样性定律、Good Regulator定理以及运行时验证中的trace与hyperproperty边界等理论框架。

Conclusion: 为Agentic AI系统的可审计性和合规性提供了一个形式化程度更高的评判标准，揭示了当前日志和追踪机制在法律层面的根本局限性，对AI治理和监管合规具有重要指导意义。

Abstract: Agentic AI systems generate runtime records, logs, traces, and audit artefacts, but the existence or integrity of such records does not by itself establish that legally operative oversight findings can be recovered from them. This technical report defines an evidentiary-adequacy criterion for a bounded class of determinations: binary findings of fact about specific events and their relations, such as whether protected data crossed a boundary, whether a human could intervene, whether an information barrier held, or whether delegated authority was valid at the moment of use.
  The criterion states that a runtime record can answer such a determination only if it carries both a typing that maps recorded events to the legally operative category and the relation, such as provenance, authority, derivation, or temporal validity, on which the determination's truth depends. The claim is one of necessity, not sufficiency.
  The report instantiates the criterion against selected EU AI Act oversight obligations and explains why tamper-proof logs, generic process frameworks, and provenance structures alone cannot establish the relevant findings. It further relates the argument to requisite variety, the Good Regulator Theorem, and the trace-versus-hyperproperty boundary of runtime verification. Companion materials and the experiment protocol are archived on Zenodo.

</details>


### [230] [Corporate sponsorship of computer science conferences: trends, structural insights, and a novel approach to ranking conferences](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01113)
*Yongzhen Wang*

Main category: cs.CY

TL;DR: 本文通过构建会议-企业赞助网络，首次系统分析了2000-2024年间计算机科学会议的企业赞助格局，并利用网络排序算法提出了一种基于赞助关系评估会议质量的新方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管企业赞助在计算机科学会议中日益普遍，但缺乏对其格局的定量理解，以及学术界与赞助企业之间互动关系的系统分析。

Method: 收集25年间高影响力计算机科学会议的赞助数据，构建会议-企业赞助网络，通过模块度优化分析网络拓扑结构，并采用基于网络的排序算法评估会议质量。

Result: 揭示了赞助网络的演化趋势和关键节点；提出的评估方法在三个主流排名系统中得到验证，展现了实用性，并突出了学术界与工业界对不同领域关注度的差异。

Conclusion: 企业赞助网络为会议评估提供了新视角，对计算机科学的学术交流格局具有重要启示，尤其是工业界已成为该学科研究的主要消费者。

Abstract: Corporate sponsorship is increasingly prevalent at computer science conferences. However, a quantitative understanding of this phenomenon has yet to be established, let alone insights into the interplay between academic conferences and sponsoring corporations, or how to leverage it. To fill these gaps, this study first explores the landscape of corporate sponsorship across a wide range of high-profile computer science conferences, shedding light on its evolution over a 25-year period from 2000 to 2024. The complex and expansive relationships between these conferences and their corporate sponsors are then systematically organized into a network for structural analysis and conference evaluation. Specifically, after modularity optimization, the network's topological properties are analyzed to identify key conferences and corporations that shape the overall structure, connectivity, and functionality. More importantly, this study makes the first attempt to employ a conference-corporation sponsorship network, along with a network-based ranking algorithm, to evaluate computer science conferences, introducing a new perspective on assessing their quality or reputation from the standpoint of corporate sponsorship. The proposed evaluation approach is benchmarked against three popular ranking systems, demonstrating not only its practical usefulness but also its unique ability to highlight the disparity in the attention that academia and industry direct to different fields of computer science. This paper has significant implications for scholarly communication in computer science, particularly as industry has become the primary consumer of academic research in the discipline.

</details>


<div id='q-fin.ST'></div>

# q-fin.ST [[Back]](#toc)

### [231] [End-to-End Parametric Portfolio Policies for Cross-Asset Futures Timing: When Do AI Models Beat Simple Rules?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00475)
*Austin Pollok,Kevin Robik*

Main category: q-fin.ST

TL;DR: 本文研究了一种端到端的AI投资策略，直接将市场状态映射到资产组合权重，使用可微夏普比率损失函数在16种流动性最强的CME期货上训练，并与等权重、风险平价和时间序列动量等规则策略进行比较。LSTM和Transformer架构在样本外表现相当，但考虑交易成本后，Transformer交易更少、表现更优。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统方法先预测收益再优化权重，存在级联误差问题。本文探索是否能通过端到端AI策略直接学习从市场状态到组合权重的映射，超越简单的规则型策略。

Method: 采用可微夏普比率作为损失函数，在16种高流动性CME期货上训练LSTM和Transformer网络，直接输出资产组合权重，与等权重、风险平价和时序动量策略进行对比。

Result: 学习策略在整体跨资产组合和多个子类别上优于规则策略；LSTM和Transformer样本外表现相当，但考虑交易成本后Transformer交易频率更低，在中等成本下仍能匹配或超越等权重策略。

Conclusion: 端到端AI投资策略在流动性充足的市场中具有竞争力，Transformer在平衡收益与交易成本方面优于LSTM，但并非所有资产类别上都一致优于规则策略。

Abstract: Timing-based tilts across asset classes can drive much of the risk and return of a diversified cross-asset portfolio. The standard approach forecasts returns and then optimizes weights. We instead study an end-to-end AI-based policy that maps market states directly to portfolio weights, and we then ask when this one-step modeling approach outperforms simple rules-based strategies. We train these policies on the sixteen most liquid CME futures, where an edge is unlikely to be due to illiquidity, using a differentiable Sharpe ratio loss function, and we benchmark them against equal weighting, risk parity, and time-series momentum. The learned policies rank above the rules on the pooled cross-asset portfolio and in several sub-asset classes, but not uniformly. In gross terms, an LSTM and a transformer-based architecture perform comparably out-of-sample, but diverge when we consider transaction costs. The transformer generates the stronger learned policy, trades far less than the LSTM, and matches or exceeds equal weighting through moderate cost.

</details>


<div id='q-fin.TR'></div>

# q-fin.TR [[Back]](#toc)

### [232] [When large trades are not news: Liquidity tail risk and price discovery](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01198)
*Umut Çetin,Mingwei Lin,Giulia Livieri*

Main category: q-fin.TR

TL;DR: 本文研究在非对称信息下，流动性供应商无法区分大额交易是知情交易还是流动性冲击。重尾流动性需求（如厚尾分布）会削弱大额交易的信息含量，使价格冲击变平缓、学习速度变慢。通过固定点方程和尾控制紧集方法，刻画了流动性尾风险作为市场冲击、价差恢复和交易信息性的关键状态变量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典模型中通常假设流动性需求（噪音交易）呈高斯分布，但现实中流动性需求可能具有厚尾特征。本文旨在回答：大额交易何时是新闻（信息驱动），何时是流动性冲击？流动性需求的尾部特征如何影响大额交易的信号解读、价格发现和市场微观结构？

Method: 构建了一个连续时间竞争性限价订单簿模型，流动性供应商观测到总订单流但无法分解为知情需求和流动性需求。流动性需求建模为Student-t分布（厚尾）。通过固定点方程求解边际成本曲线，在尾控制紧类上构造均衡。利用规则变差渐近分析研究大额订单的价格冲击。

Result: 1) 薄尾噪音下大额失衡很快被解读为信息；厚尾流动性需求下大额失衡仍可被视为流动性驱动。2) 流动性尾歧义使价格冲击变平缓、凹化，减慢了从订单流中学习的速度，延迟逆向选择溢价下降。3) 重尾改变了均衡数学结构：高斯单调性和紧性论证失效，需用尾控制紧类。4) 流动性尾越厚，价格发现越慢。5) 大额订单冲击服从规则变差渐近，指数依赖于流动性尾指数、知情竞争和后验信念。

Conclusion: 流动性尾风险是市场冲击、价差恢复和大额交易信息性的核心状态变量。模型为理解厚尾流动性需求下的市场微观结构提供了理论基础，解释了为何有些大额交易不具信息性。

Abstract: When is a large trade news, and when is it a liquidity shock? We study this question in a sequential competitive limit order book with asymmetric information. In our model, liquidity suppliers observe aggregate order flow but not its decomposition into informed demand and uninformed liquidity demand. We model uninformed order flow with Student-$t$ tails, interpreted as a reduced form for rare liquidity regimes. The tail index of liquidity demand determines how informative large trades are. With thin-tailed noise, large order imbalances are quickly interpreted as private information. With heavy-tailed liquidity demand, the same imbalances remain plausibly liquidity-driven. This liquidity-tail ambiguity flattens and concavifies price impact, slows learning from order flow, and delays the decline of adverse-selection premia. We characterize equilibrium through a fixed-point equation for the marginal-cost schedule. Heavy-tailed liquidity demand changes the mathematics of equilibrium: the Gaussian monotonicity and compactness arguments fail because remote liquidity states remain pricing-relevant at polynomial order. We construct fixed points on a tail-controlled compact class and study learning and large-order asymptotics along selected monotone branches. Repeated order flow reveals the fundamental value under stable information-rate conditions, but heavier liquidity tails slow finite-horizon price discovery. Large-order impact obeys regular-variation asymptotics whose exponents depend on the liquidity-tail index, informed competition, and posterior beliefs. The model identifies liquidity tail risk as a state variable for market impact, spread resilience, and the informativeness of large trades.

</details>
